--- layout: default title: "BigTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Text Strings" parent: "Fuzzing" --- BigTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Text Strings

BigTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Text Strings

This module is designed to respond with a single TXT record containing any number of labels, each with an arbitrary size.

This flexibility allows for generating very large DNS responses, up to the maximum allowable DNS packet size of 65535 bytes.

In this variant, the labels are composed of random ASCII text.

Category: Fuzzing

RFCs: RFC1035, RFC1464

Format

bigtxt.<LABELS>.<SIZE>.yourdomain.com

Where:

  • The <LABELS> parameter specifies the number of labels to be included in the TXT record.

  • The <SIZE> parameter specifies the number of bytes in each label. Note that the maximum possible size for a TXT label is 255 bytes as per DNS implementation.

Examples

In this example, we request to produce a TXT record containing a single label consisting of 50 random ASCII characters:

# dig bigtxt.1.50.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigtxt.1.50.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 37895
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigtxt.1.50.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:
bigtxt.1.50.yourdomain.com. 60	IN	TXT	"b56v51y6ljg76rbygrd5k0ajjwjthrrs0bxqrt10q3cb74t8u0"

;; Query time: 4 msec
;; SERVER: 127.0.0.1#53(127.0.0.1) (UDP)
;; WHEN: Fri Jan 03 09:28:45 +04 2025
;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 107

Download PCAP File


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record containing a single label consisting of 255 random ASCII characters, which is the maximum allowable size for a TXT label:

# dig bigtxt.1.255.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigtxt.1.255.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 63818
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigtxt.1.255.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:
bigtxt.1.255.yourdomain.com. 60	IN	TXT	"t67obr1l63qqbfjm79glh888m0zgypt9l3nl8w7v2h7jopk5cb20llotcmjjxfeuqbh7gvq3sw4opfske1qpts827qei5nmvzqobol571zjrhlz6peg1resetaldmka1gmqbft65bb0b8wdmyq9u027dusr27qgsepa3cjehsyq6knd1vo8skdswprv0nuqg96g1u7z4fk8cv5zn8c5ao5pxyqqjxdd4lcpibzk156xp8ihkb8m7l0hf74r9u8c"

;; Query time: 4 msec
;; SERVER: 127.0.0.1#53(127.0.0.1) (UDP)
;; WHEN: Fri Jan 03 09:28:47 +04 2025
;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 313

Download PCAP File

;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 567

Download PCAP File

Note that there is no limit on the number of labels. The only restriction is the maximum DNS packet size of 65535 bytes.


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record with 10000 labels, each containing a single random ASCII character:

Download PCAP File


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record with 10 labels, each containing 20 random ASCII characters:

# dig bigtxt.10.20.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigtxt.10.20.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd

;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 12330

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigtxt.10.20.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:

Download PCAP File


Like other features, you can append anything to the feature name to avoid receiving cached responses from the target DNS resolver. This forces the target resolver to actively communicate with our PolarDNS server instead of responding with cached answers. Using a random number is the most effective strategy:

# dig bigtxt${RANDOM}.255.255.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
